In this transaction, money does not actually change hands until some agreed upon future date\r\nSwap Forex Trading - The most common type of forward transaction is the foreign exchange swap. The average contract length is roughly 3 months. It is used as a reference in the forex market.\r\nForex Risk aversion - Risk aversion is a kind of trading behavior exhibited by the foreign exchange market when a potentially adverse event happens which may affect market conditions.
